      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 14th century
       </b>
       . During the period 1301 to 1400 there were 229
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 76 were partial, 75 were annular (three
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 54 were total, and 24 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 7 different years: 1302, 1309, 1320, 1331, 1349, 1367, and 1396.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Dates are given using the
       <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">
        Julian calendar
       </a>
       .
      </p>
